 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Item&nbsp;2.02. Results of Operations and Financial Condition </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">On January&nbsp;26, 2017, Microsoft Corporation issued a press release announcing its financial results for the fiscal quarter ended December&nbsp;31,
2016. A copy of the press release is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 to this report. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:9pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">In accordance with General Instruction B.2 of Form <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</FONT> the information in this Current Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</FONT> including Exhibit 99.1, shall not be deemed to be &#147;filed&#148; for purposes of Section&nbsp;18 of the Securities
Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#147;Exchange Act&#148;), or otherwise subject to the liability of that section, and shall not be incorporated by reference into any registration statement or other document filed under the Securities Act of
1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Item&nbsp;9.01. Financial Statements and
Exhibits </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">(d) Exhibits: </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:13pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Microsoft Cloud Strength Highlights Second Quarter Results </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>Commercial cloud annualized revenue run rate exceeds
$14.0&nbsp;billion </I></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>REDMOND, Wash. &#151; January</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;26, 2017 &#151; </B>Microsoft Corp. today announced the
following results for the quarter ended December&nbsp;31, 2016: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue was $24.1&nbsp;billion GAAP, and $26.1&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Operating income was $6.2&nbsp;billion GAAP, and $8.2&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Net income was $5.2&nbsp;billion GAAP, and $6.5&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Diluted earnings per share was $0.66 GAAP, and $0.83 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft completed the acquisition of LinkedIn Corporation (&#147;LinkedIn&#148;) on December&nbsp;8, 2016. Financial results from the acquired
business are reported in the Productivity and Business Processes segment. For the second quarter of fiscal year 2017, the results of LinkedIn, including amortization of acquired intangible assets, contributed revenue, operating income, net income,
and diluted earnings per share of $228&nbsp;million, $(201) million, $(100) million, and $(0.01), respectively. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#147;Our customers
are seeing greater value and opportunity as we partner with them through their digital transformation,&#148; said Satya Nadella, chief executive officer at Microsoft. &#147;Accelerating advancements in AI across our platforms and services will
provide further opportunity to drive growth in the Microsoft Cloud.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">The following table reconciles our financial results
reported in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (&#147;GAAP&#148;) to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial results. Microsoft has provided this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial
information to aid investors in better understanding the company&#146;s performance. Additional information regarding our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> definition is provided below. All growth comparisons relate to the
corresponding period in the last fiscal year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" ALIGN="center">

quarter of fiscal year 2017. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#147;I am pleased with our results this quarter. We see strong demand for our cloud-based services and
are executing well on our long-term growth strategy,&#148; said Amy Hood, executive vice president and chief financial officer at Microsoft. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Acquisitions and Divestitures </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Microsoft completed the acquisition of LinkedIn on December&nbsp;8, 2016 and the sale of its feature phone business in November 2016. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666"><B>Business Outlook </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft will provide forward-looking guidance in connection with this quarterly earnings
announcement on its earnings conference call and webcast. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Webcast Details </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Satya Nadella, chief executive officer, Amy Hood, executive vice president and chief financial officer, Frank Brod, chief accounting officer, John
Seethoff, deputy general counsel and corporate secretary, and Chris Suh, general manager of Investor Relations, will host a conference call and webcast at 2:30 p.m. Pacific time (5:30 p.m. Eastern time) today to discuss details of the company&#146;s
performance for the quarter and certain forward-looking information. The session may be accessed at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">http://www.microsoft.com/en-us/investor.</FONT> The webcast will be available for replay through the close of
business on January&nbsp;26, 2018. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>&#147;As Adjusted&#148; Financial Results and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
Measures </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">During the second quarter of fiscal years 2017 and 2016, GAAP revenue, operating income, net income, and diluted earnings
per share include the net impact from Windows 10 revenue deferrals. During the second quarter of fiscal year 2017, GAAP revenue, operating income, net income, and diluted earnings per share include the results of LinkedIn. These items are defined
below. In addition to these financial results reported in accordance with GAAP, Microsoft has provided certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial information to aid investors in better understanding the company&#146;s
performance. Presenting these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures gives additional insight into operational performance and helps clarify trends affecting the company&#146;s business. For comparability of reporting, management
considers this information in conjunction with GAAP amounts in evaluating business performance. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>Net Impact from Windows 10 Revenue
Deferrals.</I> With respect to our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures related to Windows 10 revenue, we believe these measures bridge investor information and minimize potential confusion during the brief period between the
time Windows 10 revenue recognition moved from upfront to ratable, and the adoption of the new revenue standard, when Windows 10 will again be recognized predominantly upfront. The net change in Windows 10 revenue from period to period is indicative
of the net change in revenue we expect from adoption of the new revenue standard. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>LinkedIn Results.</I> With respect to our <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure related to LinkedIn results, we believe this measure will help investors compare actual results for the second quarter of fiscal year 2017 to the guidance previously provided for the quarter, which
excluded LinkedIn. We do not anticipate providing this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure in the future as our guidance will incorporate expected results for LinkedIn. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">These <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to, the
measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Definitions </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>Net Impact from Windows 10 Revenue Deferrals.</I> Microsoft recorded net revenue deferrals of $2.0&nbsp;billion during the second quarter of
fiscal year 2017 and net revenue deferrals of $1.7&nbsp;billion during the second quarter of fiscal year 2016, related to Windows 10. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">With the launch of Windows 10 in July 2015, Windows 10 customers receive future versions and updates at no additional charge. Under current
revenue recognition accounting guidance, when standalone software is sold with future upgrade rights, revenue must be deferred over the life of the computing device on which it is installed. This is different from prior versions of Windows, which
were sold without upgrade rights, where all revenue from original equipment manufacturer (&#147;OEM&#148;) customers was recognized at the time of billing, i.e., upfront. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">When Microsoft adopts the new revenue standard, predominantly all Windows OEM revenue will be recognized at the time of billing, which is similar
to the revenue recognition for prior versions of Windows. Additional information regarding the new revenue standard is provided in the &#147;Recent Accounting Guidance Not Yet Adopted&#148; section of Microsoft&#146;s Form <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-Q</FONT> for the quarter ended December&nbsp;31, 2016 (Notes to Financial Statements). Microsoft reflects the recognition of Windows 10 revenue at the time of billing in &#147;As Adjusted for Windows 10 Revenue
Deferrals <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(non-GAAP)&#148;</FONT> revenue to provide comparability during the short period where Windows 10 will be recognized over the estimated life of a device, i.e., ratable, rather than at the time of billing.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>LinkedIn Results. </I>For the second quarter of fiscal year 2017, LinkedIn contributed revenue, operating income, net income, and
diluted earnings per share of $228&nbsp;million, $(201) million, $(100) million, and $(0.01), respectively. Microsoft excludes the results of LinkedIn and reflects the recognition of Windows 10 revenue at the time of billing in &#147;As Further
Adjusted for Windows 10 Revenue Deferrals, Excluding LinkedIn Results <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(non-GAAP)&#148;</FONT> to help investors compare results for the second quarter of fiscal year 2017 to the guidance previously provided for the
quarter, which excluded LinkedIn. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Constant Currency </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft presents constant currency information to provide a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> framework for assessing how our
underlying businesses performed excluding the effect of foreign currency rate fluctuations. To present this information, current and comparative prior period <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> results for entities reporting in
currencies other than United States dollars are converted into United States dollars using the average exchange rates from the comparative period rather than the actual exchange rates in effect during the respective periods. The <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented below should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to, the measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. All growth comparisons relate to the
corresponding period in the last fiscal year. </FONT></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Commercial Cloud Annualized Revenue Run Rate </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Commercial cloud annualized revenue run rate is calculated by taking revenue in the final month of the quarter multiplied by twelve for Office 365
commercial, Azure, Dynamics 365, and other cloud properties. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>About Microsoft </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft (Nasdaq &#147;MSFT&#148; @microsoft) is the leading platform and productivity company for the mobile-first, cloud-first world and its
mission is to empower every person and every organization on the planet to achieve more. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Forward-Looking Statements </B></FONT></P>
